    </td>    <td width="27" valign="top" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:20.25pt;">    <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>    </td>    <td width="329" valign="top" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:246.6pt;">    <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 20.0pt;text-indent:-10.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Secretary and General Counsel</font></p>    </td>   </tr>  </table>

<body lang="EN-US">

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">EXHIBIT&nbsp;99.1</font></b></p>

<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">KROGER REPORTS FIRST QUARTER 2010
RESULTS</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Identical
Supermarket Sales Increased 2.4% without Fuel</font></i></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Confirms Fiscal
2010 Guidance</font></i></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">CINCINNATI, Ohio, June&nbsp;17, 2010
&#151; The Kroger Co. (NYSE: KR) today reported total sales, including fuel,
increased 8.7% to $24.8 billion in the first quarter of fiscal 2010 compared
with $22.8 billion for the same period last year.&#160; Excluding fuel sales, total sales increased
3.1% in the first quarter, which ended May&nbsp;22, 2010, over the same period
last year.&#160; Identical supermarket sales,
without fuel, increased 2.4% in the first quarter over the same period last
year.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="layout-grid-mode:char;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Net earnings for the first
quarter totaled $373.7 million, or $0.58 per diluted share.&#160; Net earnings in the same period last year
were $435.1 million, or $0.66 per diluted share.</font></p>

<p style="layout-grid-mode:char;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="layout-grid-mode:char;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;I am pleased with the strong
positive identical sales growth we achieved in the first quarter while striking
a better balance on margin investments.&#160;
Our Customer 1</font><font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">st</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;strategy continues to deliver results through
improvements in all four key areas we target:&#160;
our people, our products, the overall shopping experience in our stores,
and prices,&#148; said David B. Dillon, Kroger&#146;s chairman and chief executive
officer.&#160; &#147;As a result, the total number
of families we serve continues to grow and our most loyal customers are buying
more with us.&#148;</font></p>

<p style="layout-grid-mode:char;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="layout-grid-mode:char;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Details of First Quarter 2010
Results</font></u></b></p>

<p style="layout-grid-mode:char;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="layout-grid-mode:char;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Including Kroger&#146;s retail
fuel operations, FIFO gross margin (Table 1) was 22.66% of sales for the first
quarter of fiscal 2010, a decrease of 168 basis points compared to the first
quarter last year.&#160; Excluding retail fuel
operations, FIFO gross margin decreased 77 basis points.&#160; Supermarket selling gross margin (Table 1)
declined 71 basis points without fuel.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="layout-grid-mode:char;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="layout-grid-mode:char;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">1<a name="PB_1_053433_7056"></a></font></p>

<div style="layout-grid-mode:char;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='1',FILE='C:\JMS\mweinst\10-12169-1\task4155230\12169-1-mm-01.htm',USER='mweinst',CD='Jun 17 07:37 2010' -->


<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p align="center" style="layout-grid-mode:char;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="layout-grid-mode:char;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Kroger recorded a $15.4
million LIFO charge during the quarter, a decrease of $7.7 million from the
same period last year.&#160; Excluding retail
fuel operations, the LIFO charge decreased 4 basis points as a percentage of
sales.</font></p>

<p style="layout-grid-mode:char;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="layout-grid-mode:char;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Including Kroger&#146;s retail fuel
operations, operating, general and administrative (OG&amp;A) costs were 16.95%
of sales, a decline of 72 basis points compared with the first quarter last
year.&#160; Excluding retail fuel operations,
OG&amp;A increased 13 basis points from the same period last year as a result
of higher health care and pension costs, and credit card fees.&#160; These rising expenses were mostly offset by
identical supermarket sales leverage and the benefit from productivity
improvements, process changes, and Kroger&#146;s efforts to reduce energy usage.</font></p>

<p style="layout-grid-mode:char;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="layout-grid-mode:char;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Financial Strategy</font></u></b></p>

<p style="layout-grid-mode:char;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="layout-grid-mode:char;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Capital investment, excluding
acquisitions and purchases of leased facilities, totaled $532.2 million for the
first quarter, compared with $621.8 million for the same period last year.</font></p>

<p style="layout-grid-mode:char;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="layout-grid-mode:char;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Net total debt (Table 5) was
$7.1 billion, a decrease of $339.8 million from a year ago.&#160; On a rolling four-quarters basis, Kroger&#146;s
net total debt to EBITDA ratio, adjusted for the southern California impairment
charge in fiscal 2009 and Hurricane Ike in fiscal 2008, was 1.91 compared with 1.77
during the same period last year.</font></p>

<p style="layout-grid-mode:char;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="layout-grid-mode:char;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Strong cash flow enabled
Kroger to invest $79.5 million to repurchase 3.6 million shares of stock at an
average price of $21.89 per share during the first quarter.&#160; Since the first quarter ended, Kroger
repurchased an additional 1.9 million shares of stock at an average price of
$20.25.&#160; Approximately $240 million
remains under the $1 billion stock repurchase program announced in January&nbsp;2008.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2<a name="PB_2_053459_5335"></a></font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='2',FILE='C:\JMS\mweinst\10-12169-1\task4155230\12169-1-mm-01.htm',USER='mweinst',CD='Jun 17 07:37 2010' -->


<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Fiscal
2010 Guidance</font></u></b></p>

<p style="layout-grid-mode:char;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="layout-grid-mode:char;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Kroger confirmed its
identical supermarket sales and earnings guidance for fiscal 2010.&#160; The Company said it
continues to expect identical supermarket sales growth, excluding fuel, of 2%
to 3% for the year.&#160; Net earnings are
expected to range from $1.60 to $1.80 per diluted share for the year.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="layout-grid-mode:char;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;Throughout the difficult
operating environment, the Kroger team has stayed squarely focused on
delivering on our Customer 1</font><font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">st</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;strategy.&#160; We continue to build momentum and grow market
share as we invest in our asset base and cost-saving projects.&#160; As a result, we are generating free cash flow
that strengthens our financial position and rewards shareholders through
dividends and share repurchases,&#148; Mr.&nbsp;Dillon said.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Kroger,
the nation&#146;s largest traditional grocery retailer, employs more than 334,000
associates who serve customers in 2,470 supermarkets and multi-department
stores in 31 states under two dozen local banner names including Kroger, City
Market, Dillons, Jay C, Food 4 Less, Fred Meyer, Fry&#146;s, King Soopers, QFC,
Ralphs and Smith&#146;s.&#160; The Company also
operates 779 convenience stores, 375 fine jewelry stores, 909 supermarket fuel
centers and 40 food processing plants in the U.S.&#160; Kroger, headquartered in Cincinnati, Ohio,
focuses its charitable efforts on supporting hunger relief, health and wellness
initiatives, and local organizations in the communities it serves.&#160; For more information about Kroger, please
visit www.kroger.com.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"># # #</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Note:&#160; Fuel sales have historically had a low FIFO
gross margin rate and OG&amp;A rate as compared to corresponding rates on
non-fuel sales.&#160; As a result, Kroger
discloses such rates, both including and excluding the effect of retail fuel
operations.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3<a name="PB_3_053520_5796"></a></font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This
press release contains certain forward-looking statements about the future
performance of the Company. These statements are based on management&#146;s
assumptions and beliefs in light of the information currently available to it.
Such statements are indicated by words such as &#147;confirmed,&#148; &#147;expected,&#148; and &#147;expect.&#148;&nbsp;Aggressive
competition, economic conditions, interest rates, goodwill impairment, the
success of programs designed to increase our identical supermarket sales
without fuel, and labor disputes, particularly as the Company seeks to manage
increases in health care and pension costs, could materially affect our
expected identical supermarket sales growth and earnings per share. Earnings
per share also will be affected by the number of shares outstanding and
volatility in the Company&#146;s fuel margins. Earnings and sales also may be
affected by adverse weather conditions and related climate change, particularly
to the extent that hurricanes, tornadoes, floods, and other conditions disrupt
our operations or those of our suppliers; create shortages in the availability
or increases in the cost of products that we sell in our stores or materials
and ingredients we use in our manufacturing facilities; or raise the cost of
supplying energy to our various operations, including the cost of transportation.&nbsp;
Our results also will be affected by rising commodity costs, the inconsistency
of the economic recovery, consumer confidence, and changes in inflation or
deflation in product and operating costs.&#160;
These forward-looking statements are subject to uncertainties and other
factors that could cause actual results to differ materially.&nbsp; We assume
no obligation to update the information contained herein.&#160; Please refer to Kroger&#146;s reports and filings
with the Securities and Exchange Commission for a further discussion of these
risks and uncertainties.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Note:&#160; Kroger&#146;s quarterly conference call with
investors will be broadcast live online at 10&nbsp;a.m. (ET) on June&nbsp;17,
2010 at www.kroger.com and www.streetevents.com.&#160; An on-demand replay of the webcast will be
available from approximately 1&nbsp;p.m. (ET) today through Thursday, July&nbsp;1,
2010.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"># # #</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Note:
Certain prior-year amounts have been reclassified to conform to current-year
presentation.&#160; Certain per share amounts
and percentages may not sum due to rounding.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Note:&#160; The Company defines FIFO gross margin, as
described in the earnings release, as sales minus merchandise costs, including
advertising, warehousing and transportation, but excluding the Last-In
First-Out (LIFO) charge.&#160; This measure is
included to reflect trends in current cost of product.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Note:&#160; The Company defines selling gross margin, as
described in the earnings release related to the Company&#146;s supermarkets, as
gross margin before incurring expenses directly related to distributing and
merchandising the products on its store shelves.&#160; These expenses include advertising,
warehousing, transportation, and shrink.&#160;
Selling gross margin is a measure of how competitively the Company is
pricing the products it sells.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)&#160;&#160; Merchandise costs and operating, general and administrative
expenses exclude depreciation and amortization expense and rent expense which
are included in separate expense lines.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)&#160;&#160; LIFO charges of $15.4 and $23.1 were recorded in the first quarter
of 2010 and 2009, respectively.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

</div>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.05pt;"><hr size="1" width="25%" noshade color="black" align="left"></div>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.05pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Kroger defines a
supermarket as identical when it has been open without expansion or relocation
for five full quarters.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.05pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.05pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Kroger defines a
supermarket as comparable when it has been open for five full quarters,
including expansions and relocations.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

<div>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Table 5.&#160;
Reconciliation of Total Debt to Net Total Debt</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(in millions)</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(unaudited)</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Net
total debt should not be considered an alternative to any GAAP measure of
performance or liquidity.&#160; Management
believes net total debt is an important measure of liquidity, and a primary
component of measuring compliance with the financial covenants under the
Company&#146;s credit facility.&#160; Net total
debt should be reviewed in conjunction with Kroger&#146;s financial results reported
in accordance with GAAP.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
following table provides a reconciliation of total debt to net total debt and
compares the balance in the first quarter of 2010 to the balance in the first
quarter of 2009.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
